A crash between those two commands resumes from ref R plus the provably clean L worktree/index and runs only read-tree. If L is ahead/diverged, the worktree/index is dirty, either ref is missing, or ancestry is indeterminate, checkpoint creation fails closed before candidate bytes. After commit-tree emits one lowercase commit SHA candidateCommit, run `['git','update-ref','refs/heads/main',candidateCommit,oldCommit]`, then normal non-force `['git','push','--porcelain','origin','refs/heads/main:refs/heads/main']`, then `['git','fetch','--prune','origin','refs/heads/main:refs/remotes/origin/main']`; accepted push is exit zero with exactly one parsed porcelain `ok` ref record and empty warning/error stream, while rejection/response loss always proceeds to the exact fetch. If fetched origin/main equals candidateCommit, publication succeeded. If it is a schema-valid descendant preserving the exact candidate declared-path bytes, it is the winner and convergence rules apply. If it still equals oldCommit after a proven rejected/no-effect push, the exact same candidate may retry. Any other remote is rescanned under the race rules. Local advancement/recovery is explicit: a crash after update-ref adopts only the unique hash-valid candidate child; when fetched winner is R rather than candidateCommit, run `['git','update-ref','refs/heads/main',R,candidateCommit]` followed by `['git','read-tree','--reset','-u',R]` only after the clean O/C matrix proves no undeclared dirt, then verify HEAD/index/worktree equal R before rebuilding. Convergence candidate K uses the declared two-parent commit-tree argv, the same update-ref/push/fetch sequence with expected old local winner, and no force/lease. Every command uses the closed Desk environment; stdout/stderr/exit and ref/tree/index/worktree results are persisted before phase advance. Push response loss, local-ref-update crash, fetch failure, rejected winner, and read-tree recovery are fault-tested.
- Release-provenance exposes shared `normalizeReleaseProvenanceArgv(fullArgv)` requiring exact prefix `["pnpm","release:provenance","--"]`, and both executable wrapper and in-process tests pass only the returned suffix to `createReleaseProvenanceCli(deps)`. Every Unit33-37 release-provenance ProcessSpec, not only ensures, goes through this production normalizer/API and its actual stdout/stderr/output tree before finish-command ingestion. `verify-drift` runs exact fetch/read. `ensure-qa-deploy` classifies complete Cloudflare inventory plus exact QA health; its sole mutation child is `["pnpm","run","deploy:qa"]`, and exact health SHA remains authority even when inventory returns no delta. `ensure-pr` requires exact identity head/base/title/body hash discovery and its sole mutation child is `["gh","pr","create","--repo","spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2","--head",I.branch,"--base","main","--title",I.prTitle,"--body",I.prBody]`. `merge-pr` accepts exact merged outcome or complete readiness and its sole mutation child is `["gh","pr","merge",P,"--repo","spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2","--squash","--match-head-commit",H]`. There is no alternate/admin/merge/rebase/force/auto/delete-branch/reconciliation mutator. `capture-deployments` uses the exact endpoint/schema; every GitHub adapter pins identities and classifies incomplete pagination as indeterminate.
- The two Unit37 review commands are ordered immediately after `production-visual-dogfood` and before final production cleanup. Each owns its own command-attempt out directory outside the visual runner tree and writes exactly one canonical hashed report, respectively `visual-qa-review.md` and `visual-design-review.md`; neither may edit or add a file under the immutable 38-file runner output. `VisualReviewer={role,agentId,verdict:'clean',artifactPath,reportSha256,visualArtifactSetSha256}` is no-extra-fields with role `visual_qa|design_visual`, distinct canonical lowercase UUID agentIds, the matching task-relative report path/hash, and the exact immutable runner-set hash. Unit37 cannot pass without exactly one reviewer of each role, both latest command attempts passed, both canonical reports parse/hash/cross-link, and zero open finding.
- Every Unit37 StageRun failure decision after merge is first persisted by exact derived-only `record-post-merge-disposition --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt none|A`. It writes/hashes/pushes immutable stage-owned `post-merge-failure-disposition.v1.json`, creates its own sanitized capability evidence when required, appends both hashes, refreshes continuity atomically, and is byte-idempotent; failed StageRun, disposition, and capability bytes never gain resolution fields after terminalization. `PostMergeTerminalCode` is exact `credential_missing|billing_required|platform_capability_missing|agent_runtime_unavailable|review_findings|github_rate_limited|github_5xx|cloudflare_5xx|dns_failure|network_timeout|eventual_consistency|cleanup_incomplete|spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal|sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul|exit_nonzero|warning|output_invalid|provider_indeterminate|provider_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity|validation_failed|configuration_failed|provenance_failed`. Exact no-extra-fields `PostMergeFailureDisposition={version:1,releaseRun,unit:37,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,commandMode,terminalCode,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,retryOrdinal,classification,maxRetries,runFailureReason,repairCode,createdAt}` and has no resolution member. `human_blocker` is discriminated as preflight with `attempt:null,commandMode:'preflight'` or process with positive attempt and `commandMode:'process'`; credential/billing/platform codes alone qualify, while agent runtime is external_wait. Reviewer FINDINGS is repair_successor/post_merge_finding/review_finding; provider/network ordinals 1 and 2 are transient_retry/maxRetries 2; ordinal 3+ is external_wait; cleanup_incomplete ordinals 1 and 2 retry and ordinal 3 becomes repair_successor/post_merge_repair/cleanup; ordinary code defects use the exact repair mapping. If an attempt-none preflight is available when rerun, no disposition or evidence is written and the CLI returns exact `preflight_recovered`, allowing a fresh same-unit StageRun. Retry ordinals use persisted disposition history only; wait ordinals use separate wait-checkpoint history below. Unknown/forged combinations reject without mutation.
- Post-merge disposition derivation is total over `(terminalCode,retryOrdinal,logicalName,commandMode,environmentPolicy)` and uses no default branch. Exact tuple families are: `credential_missing|billing_required|platform_capability_missing -> {classification:'human_blocker',maxRetries:0,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}`; `agent_runtime_unavailable -> {classification:'external_wait',maxRetries:2,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}` after its two journal-owned attempts; `review_findings -> {classification:'repair_successor',maxRetries:0,runFailureReason:'post_merge_finding',repairCode:'review_finding'}`; `github_rate_limited|github_5xx|cloudflare_5xx|dns_failure|network_timeout|eventual_consistency|provider_indeterminate|provider_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity|spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal -> {classification:'transient_retry',maxRetries:2,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}` for ordinals 1..2 and `{classification:'external_wait',maxRetries:2,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}` for ordinal 3+; `cleanup_incomplete -> transient_retry/maxRetries:2/nulls` for ordinals 1..2 and `repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/cleanup` for ordinal 3+; `sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul|exit_nonzero|warning|output_invalid|validation_failed -> repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/production_validation`; `configuration_failed -> repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/configuration`; and `provenance_failed -> repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/provenance`. Typed provider/credential/configuration signals take precedence over generic exit/output/process codes, so an adapter-positive capability failure never falls through to exit_nonzero. Capability binding is also total: preflight credential/platform evidence names the exact blocked CapabilityEntry and its declared probe; process `pr-ensure` maps to `github_pr_write/process:pr-ensure`, `merge-ensure` to `github_merge_write/process:merge-ensure`, QA deploy to `cloudflare_workers_edit/process:qa-deploy-ensure`, D1 cleanup/reconcile/lifecycle operations to `cloudflare_d1_edit/process:<logicalName>`, and a provider-positive Cloudflare billing response to `cloudflare_billing/process:<logicalName>`. Exact process-only capability domain is `github_pr_write|github_merge_write|cloudflare_workers_edit|cloudflare_d1_edit|cloudflare_billing`; it never appears in preflight available proofs. A terminal code/context without exactly one table row or one capability mapping is schema-invalid and writes nothing. Tests enumerate the Cartesian legal rows, every retry boundary, every illegal context, and precedence over generic process failures.
- Units32-36 use a separate pre-merge lifecycle and can never create a repair successor. Every failed stage first invokes exact derived-only `record-pre-merge-disposition --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit 32|33|34|35|36 --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt none|A`, which writes/hashes/pushes one immutable stage-owned `pre-merge-failure-disposition.v1.json` before any retry or fix. Exact no-extra-fields `PreMergeFailureDisposition={version:1,releaseRun,unit:32|33|34|35|36,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,commandMode,terminalCode,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,classification,retryOrdinal,maxRetries,createdAt}` uses the same closed terminal-code domain, `attempt:null,commandMode:'preflight'` versus positive-attempt `commandMode:'process'|'agent'` discrimination, capability-evidence binding, and terminal-code precedence as PostMergeFailureDisposition, with `classification:'retry_same_unit'|'external_wait'|'human_blocker'|'fix_current_branch'`. Credential, billing, and platform-capability codes are human_blocker/maxRetries 0; agent-runtime unavailability is external_wait and agent mode only after its two journal-owned probes; provider/network/process transients are retry_same_unit/maxRetries 2 at ordinals 1..2 and external_wait at ordinal 3+; cleanup_incomplete is retry_same_unit at ordinals 1..2 and fix_current_branch at ordinal 3+; review findings (agent mode only), sanitizer/output/warning/exit, validation, configuration, and provenance failures are fix_current_branch/maxRetries 0. Unknown tuples reject. Before `set-merge-sha`, Unit36 is pre-merge and obeys this same matrix, but fix_current_branch is legal only after an authoritative complete observation proves the PR unmerged and no merge effect; an absent/indeterminate observation can only retry or wait; after `set-merge-sha` it can only reconcile/pass as specified below. retry_same_unit appends a fresh same-unit StageRun at unchanged HEAD; external_wait uses resume-external-wait; human_blocker uses exact resolve-pre-merge-blocker, which writes a separate immutable capability resolution and resumes the same unit only after a fresh successful read-only probe; fix_current_branch authorizes a tracked fix on the current branch, after which the old ReleaseRun is atomically superseded and the next ReleaseRun restarts at Unit32. No Unit32-36 path writes post-merge disposition/repair files, initializes a successor, or enters repaired release-terminal.
- A repair_successor never reruns the defective tree without a reviewed repair. After the failed Unit37 stage disposition or passed-Unit37 terminal disposition push, Work Merger invokes strict measured `pnpm release:terminal -- --mode successor` actions. Exact `RepairBrief={code,artifactPath,artifactSha256,reviewerRole,promptSha256,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,affectedSurfaces}` retains finite code `review_finding|provenance|cleanup|configuration|production_validation`; `affectedSurfaces={ui:boolean,api:boolean,migrationConfig:boolean}` is derived from the failed command/artifact registry and cannot be caller-supplied. The sole exact `PostMergeSuccessorAttempt`, suite-attempt, phase/null, runtime-wait, and implementation-evidence schemas are the Round 52 declarations below. The successor doing doc contains implementation-only units and excludes Units32-37. Crash recovery validates/completes or interrupts one bounded suite attempt before a fresh ordinal, never skips or duplicates a phase. Only implementation_complete may initialize the successor manifest and run universal Units32-37 once, followed by its PR/merge/production/terminal/archive/index flow.
- Successor completion evidence is a closed registry, never an arbitrary path/hash collection. Exact `SuccessorImplementationRegistry={version:1,successorKey,doingPath,doingSha256,groups,reviewRoles,createdAt}` has BINARY-sorted unique `groups:{groupId,testUnitId,implementationUnitId,verificationUnitId}[]` parsed from the approved successor doing doc: every implementation group appears exactly once as contiguous status-bearing `a` test, `b` implementation, and `c` verification headers with What/Output/Acceptance; no other implementation unit shape is legal. `reviewRoles` is the BINARY-sorted set containing `implementation`, `migration_config`, `security_privacy`, and `test`, plus `design_visual` iff RepairBrief.affectedSurfaces.ui and `api_compatibility` iff RepairBrief.affectedSurfaces.api; therefore the only legal global order is the applicable subsequence of `api_compatibility|design_visual|implementation|migration_config|security_privacy|test`. migration_config remains required and records clean no-impact when unaffected. `SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt={version:1,successorKey,unitId,phase:'test'|'implementation'|'verification',status:'completed',sourceBaseSha,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,redEvidencePath,redEvidenceSha256,commands,artifactPaths,artifactSetSha256,completedAt}` exists exactly once for every registry unit. All sourceHeadSha/treeSha equal the final clean pushed implementation head/tree and sourceBaseSha equals implementationBaseSha; test phase alone has nonnull immutable red evidence proving its expected nonzero assertion before implementation, while implementation/verification have both red fields null. `commands:{argv,expected:'red'|'green',exitCode,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount}[]` is nonempty: test has at least one red command with exitCode 1..255 and then its final green replay; all other expected green commands have exitCode zero; every warningCount is zero. `SuccessorReviewReport={version:1,successorKey,role,agentId,verdict:'clean',sourceHeadSha,treeSha,completedAt}` exists exactly once for every registry reviewRole with distinct canonical agent ids. `SuccessorVerificationArtifact={version:1,successorKey,unitId,command,exitCode:0,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount:0,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,createdAt}` exists at least once for every verification unit and exactly matches its receipt commands/artifacts. Implementation evidence arrays must be the BINARY-sorted normalized task-relative paths of these exact closed sets; all bytes schema/hash-validate, all unit IDs/roles equal the registry with no omission/extra/duplicate, every source/tree equals the final implementation head/tree, every group is complete, and every set hash covers compact canonical `{path,sha256}[]` with no final LF. `reviewReportPaths` points to the complete projected SuccessorReviewReport bytes; the enclosing `{path,sha256}` review set supplies the only report hashes, so no report self-hashes. The registry path is exact task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/implementation-registry.v1.json`; unit receipts/red evidence live only under `artifacts/post-merge-successor/units/`, review reports only under `artifacts/post-merge-successor/reviews/`, verification artifacts only under `artifacts/post-merge-successor/verification/`, and coverage only under its declared sibling directory. Every one is appended to the successor manifest as an Artifact before implementation evidence, so terminal ordinary-file validation sees no task-root extras.
- Changed coverage scope is derived independently from coverage instrumentation and retained as an exact closed artifact set. Exact no-extra-fields `CoveragePathSet={version:1,kind:'diff'|'production_executable'|'instrumented',paths,pathsSha256,createdAt}` uses BINARY-sorted unique repo-relative paths and hashes compact canonical `paths` bytes with no final LF. The sole basenames under task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/coverage/` are `coverage-diff-paths.json`, `coverage-production-executables.json`, `coverage-instrumented-paths.json`, `coverage-scope.json`, `coverage-total.json`, `coverage-changed.json`, `coverage-command-results.json`, and `coverage-summary.json`. Exact no-extra-fields `CoverageScope={version:1,diffPathSetPath,diffPathSetSha256,productionExecutablePathSetPath,productionExecutablePathSetSha256,instrumentedPathSetPath,instrumentedPathSetSha256,changedExecutablePaths,changedExecutableSetSha256,allChangedExecutablePathsInstrumented:true,createdAt}` cross-hashes the first three files. `CoverageTotal={version:1,metrics,createdAt}` carries exact CoverageMetricSet. `CoverageChanged={version:1,changed,coverageScopePath,coverageScopeSha256,createdAt}` carries exact ChangedCoverage and hashes CoverageScope. `CoverageCommandSet={version:1,commands,createdAt}` carries the exact nonempty zero-warning CoverageSummary command array. `diff` is exact `git diff --name-only implementationBaseSha...implementationHeadSha`. The independent production registry is every tracked regular file matching `app/**/*.{ts,tsx}`, `workers/**/*.{ts,tsx}`, or `scripts/**/*.{ts,mts,mjs}`, plus present root files `vite.config.ts`, `vitest.config.ts`, `playwright.config.ts`, and `react-router.config.ts`, minus `**/*.d.ts` and exact path segments `test`, `tests`, `__tests__`, `fixtures`, `generated`, `node_modules`, `coverage`, and build-output directories; classification never reads instrumentation. changedExecutablePaths is the intersection of diff and production paths; every member must occur in the independent instrumented set. For both measured and not_applicable, changedExecutableSetSha256 hashes compact canonical changedExecutablePaths bytes. Measured is required for a nonempty set and reports positive 100% metrics over exactly it; not_applicable requires an empty set and the hash of exact bytes `[]`. `coverage-summary.json` contains exact CoverageSummary and is the sole value legal for PostMergeImplementationEvidence.coverageSummaryPath at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/coverage/coverage-summary.json`; CoverageSummary.artifacts is exactly the BINARY-sorted seven-entry subordinate `{path,sha256}` set for every other basename in that directory, excludes the summary itself to avoid a self-hash, and permits no substitution or extras; its commands, total, and changed members byte-equal the command, total, and changed artifact payloads. Every path/hash cross-link, set membership, classifier exclusion, metric, and no-extra-fields boundary is independently validated.
- The predecessor remains validating/unarchived until the successor receipt and generation-aware index are pushed/read back. The successor Work Merger then invokes repair-intermediate release-terminal at positive predecessor depth or repair-root release-terminal at depth zero. Release-terminal alone owns exact no-extra-fields `PredecessorSupersedeAttempt={version:1,predecessorIdentitySha256,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationLocator,successorArchiveValidationSha256,predecessorTaskPath,predecessorDoingLocator,predecessorTaskArchivePath,successorJournalSha256,repairLinkSha256,terminalCleanupSha256,phase,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,startedAt,updatedAt}` with phase `prepared|lifecycle_done|root_moved|validated`. Every immutable identity/path/input-hash/start field is nonnull in every phase; only the three derived lifecycle result hashes follow the null matrix below. Prepared has `taskDoneSha256`, `doingDoneSha256`, and `trackLandedRowSha256` null; lifecycle_done adds the two done hashes only; root_moved adds the Landed-row hash; validated preserves all fields and proves the source absent, target present, and final candidate parse/hash-valid. Each transition advances exactly once, `updatedAt` increases canonically, no field may regress or drift, and only validated may replace the attempt with final exact no-extra-fields `PredecessorSupersedeReceipt={version:1,predecessorIdentitySha256,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationLocator,successorArchiveValidationSha256,repairLinkSha256,terminalCleanupSha256,taskSourcePath,taskArchivePath,doingLocator,prNumber,prUrl,validatorMergeSha,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,sourceAbsent:true,targetPresent:true,archiveValid:true,completedAt}` at registered basename `predecessor-supersede.v1.json`. The receipt locator/hash inputs resolve uniquely through their declared domains; `doingLocator` is the stable TaskDocumentLocator below; PR/merge/identity bytes equal the repair leaf and predecessor lineage contracts. The terminal checkpoint atomically creates and reads back the receipt while deleting the attempt; partial receipt, retained attempt, illegal null matrix, skipped phase, changed source bytes, or alternate path fails closed. Lifecycle changes predecessor task validating->done, clears iterations.active, records superseded history and exact successor task/PR/merge links, changes predecessor doing VALIDATING->COMPLETE, lands only the predecessor track row, and archives through the same Git matrix. A predecessor is terminal only after this receipt and its ArchiveValidationReceipt are pushed/read back. A legal transient appends a fresh Unit37 StageRun at unchanged mergeSha and carries the disposition/retry ordinal; it never reopens or mutates the failed StageRun. The all-the-way-through mandate continues through every successor in the same invocation.
- Before predecessor supersede preparation, release-terminal runs the host-bound TerminalCleanup protocol with the successor receipt as the special authorization replacing normal passed-Unit37 authorization. It builds the validator/runtime at the immutable repair leaf PostMergeRepairReceipt's `validatorMergeSha`, while original `mergeSha`/`branchHeadSha` are used only for ancestry, ref, and worktree cleanup and proof of original worktree/ref absence. Prepared supersede also freezes exact `PostMergeRepairLink={version:1,dispositionKind,successorKey,successorTaskPath,successorReceiptPath,successorReceiptSha256,successorPrNumber,successorPrUrl,successorMergeSha,predecessorTaskPath,predecessorReleaseRun,predecessorReleaseStatus,predecessorMergeSha,sourceDispositionPath,sourceDispositionSha256,repairBriefSha256s,completedAt}`. dispositionKind is `stage|terminal`; stage requires predecessorReleaseStatus failed and source PostMergeFailureDisposition, while terminal requires predecessorReleaseStatus passed and source TerminalFailureDisposition. At lifecycle_done it atomically writes `post-merge-repair-link.v1.json`, hash-verifies then removes `post-merge-successor.attempt.v1.json`, and records both hashes in the supersede attempt. Prepared hashes the existing successor journal and TerminalCleanup plus the frozen repair-link candidate, so successorJournalSha256, repairLinkSha256, and terminalCleanupSha256 are nonempty and immutable in every phase.
- Repaired closure archive validation is the explicit second semantic branch of `--mode archive`: normal tasks require a passed ReleaseRun and DeskArchive; repair-intermediate and repair-root tasks require either one failed `post_merge_finding|post_merge_repair` ReleaseRun with a stage-kind link, or one passed ReleaseRun with no final terminal receipt plus a terminal-kind link to a repair_successor TerminalFailureDisposition; both require execution-contract-exact PostMergeRepairLink, original TerminalCleanup, task/history outcome superseded, and PredecessorSupersedeReceipt. Its task terminal protocol closed set is exactly `terminal-cleanup.v1.json`, `post-merge-repair-link.v1.json`, `predecessor-supersede.v1.json`, `track-disposition.v1.json`, and `archive-validation.v1.json`; no handoff/supersede attempt remains. The execution-contract-exact PredecessorSupersedeReceipt is written as `predecessor-supersede.v1.json`. After predecessor archive, the same semantic TrackDisposition/conditional generation-qualified TrackArchive/final archive-validation flow runs with the predecessor identity as trigger; this may finally archive the track that the still-validating predecessor kept active. Logical cross-task receipt fields are stable locators and resolve through the unique active root, task archive, or TrackArchive target receipt. A predecessor is terminal only after its archive validation receipt is pushed/read back and its validator runtime/archive are absent. Unit29.2 tests every phase/race/recovery/classifier/closed-set branch; a typed transient appends a fresh Unit37 StageRun under its retry cap, while a typed capability blocker performs no mutation. The same Work Merger invocation continues through every repair successor until predecessor closure.
- Evidence is a unit-discriminated no-extra-fields union. `Reviewer={role,agentId,verdict:'clean',artifactPath,reportSha256,promptSha256}` is exact with finite role, lowercase UUID agentId, and matching passed AgentCommand hashes. `Deployment={id,createdAt,source:'github_actions'|'wrangler'|'dashboard'|'unknown'|null}` has nonempty id/canonical time; provider text maps only to that finite classification and is never retained. `Health=HealthSuccess|HealthFailure` records every scheduled sample through the exact closed schemas below. `Cleanup={outcomePath,phaseEvidencePaths,preDeleteRowsPath,userDeletePath,postDeleteRowsPath,retainedDoAllowlistPath,userAbsent,relationalProductRowsZero,contentBearingDoStateZero,identifierBearingDoMetadataRetained,residueClean,cleanupRecovered,cleanupIncomplete}` uses task-relative proof paths and derived flags. `Visual={baseUrl,reportPath,metricsPath,ledgerPath,screenshotPaths,visualArtifactSetSha256,cleanup,readyCount,reviewerGatedCount}` requires canonical production base, exact closed/hash-matched visual set, parsed report/metrics/ledger/Cleanup, and zero counts. `Check={name,url:CheckUrl,conclusion:'success',headSha}` requires exact PR head and the provider-discriminated URL/id binding below. `SquashCommit={sha,parents:[Sha],treeSha}` has one parent. `CiWorkflow={databaseId,runAttempt,workflowPath:'.github/workflows/ci.yml',headSha,status:'completed',conclusion:'success',url,createdAt,event:'push'}` requires positive id, expected SHA/time/url. Exact `GitHubWorkflowStatus` is `requested|queued|pending|waiting|in_progress|completed`; exact `GitHubWorkflowConclusion` is `action_required|cancelled|failure|neutral|skipped|stale|success|timed_out`, matching the GitHub workflow-run REST domain. `Workflow={databaseId,runAttempt,workflowPath:'.github/workflows/production-deploy.yml',headSha,triggeringCiDatabaseId,triggeringCiRunAttempt,status,conclusion,url,createdAt,event:'workflow_run'}` requires triggering id/run-attempt equal CiWorkflow.databaseId/runAttempt; status is one `GitHubWorkflowStatus`, conclusion is null exactly for every noncompleted status, and completed requires one `GitHubWorkflowConclusion`. `DeployJob={id,runId,runAttempt,headSha,name:'deploy',status,conclusion,url,startedAt,completedAt}` uses positive ids, merge SHA, GitHubJobUrl whose runId/jobId equal its runId/id, canonical/null times, exact GitHubJobStatus/GitHubJobConclusion, null conclusion/completedAt for every noncompleted status, null startedAt for requested/queued/pending/waiting, canonical startedAt for in_progress, and one job conclusion plus canonical completedAt and canonical/null startedAt for completed. Unknown status/conclusion strings reject, and discovery freezes first matching identity, rejects duplicates/drift, and passes only completed/success. `ProductionRelease={status:'promoted',sourceSha,runAttempt,phase:'complete',treeHash,triggeringCiDatabaseId,triggeringCiRunAttempt,reviewedMigrations:string[],migrationApply:'not_needed'|'succeeded',databaseRollbackSupported:false,previousVersionId,candidateVersionId}` is exact; triggering id/attempt equal CiWorkflow, runAttempt equals the selected Workflow runAttempt, migrations sorted/unique with matching apply state, and distinct valid Worker version IDs match health.
- Every top-level lifecycle-smoke Cleanup and nested Visual Cleanup derives from one final outcome envelope, one terminally immutable record log per executed phase, and four immutable fact proofs. Primary-only basenames are `cleanup-outcome.json`, `cleanup-phase-primary.json`, `cleanup-pre-delete-rows.json`, `cleanup-user-delete.json`, `cleanup-post-delete-rows.json`, and `cleanup-retained-do-allowlist.json`; a recovery adds `cleanup-phase-recovery.json`. Resolved paths stay inside the owning attempt `out/`; `lstat` proves regular non-symlinks and no pair shares a path or device/inode. `CleanupIdentity={userId,emailSha256,reportAttempts,purgeTargets}` uses a nonempty userId, Sha256 of the disposable email rather than raw email, and sorted unique exact `{recipeId,attemptId}` arrays with purgeTargets a subset. Lifecycle reportAttempts byte-equals A+B from `smoke-results.json` while purgeTargets is exactly B; Visual has its sole attempt in both arrays. `CleanupFailureCode` is finite `deadline|attempt_budget|cook_attempt_budget|network|rate_limited|server|protocol|identity|residue|purge|d1|user_delete|proof|sanitizer|unknown`; raw error names/codes map to `unknown`. `CleanupPass={phase,startedAt,endedAt,status,failureCode}` uses phase `primary|recovery`, status `passed|failed`, canonical times, and null failureCode iff passed. `CleanupCall={sequence,phase,at,method,status,recipeId,attemptId}` uses strictly increasing positive sequence, method `GET|DELETE`, safe-integer HTTP status `100..599`, and nullable attempt only for GET. `PurgeCompletion={recipeId,attemptId,phase,deleteCallSequence,purgeCompletedAt}` cross-links one exact target DELETE call whose status is 204 and whose at equals purgeCompletedAt; every purgeTarget has exactly one completion across all phases, every DELETE 202/204 names a purgeTarget, and any DELETE for a non-target rejects evidence. Recovery byte-verifies primary completions and never re-DELETEs an already completed target. `RetiredAttempt={recipeId,attemptId,terminalRevision,terminalStatus,terminalSnapshotSha256,replacementAttemptId,replacementStartSha256,finalResidueSha256}` is no-extra-fields and sorted by recipeId/attemptId; terminalRevision is a nonnegative safe integer, terminalStatus is `COMPLETED|ABANDONED`, hashes match unique canonical sanitized entries in the owning smoke report and phase residue, replacement start is later than terminal, and replacementAttemptId is a reportAttempt. Lifecycle has exactly one retirement for A with revision 4/status COMPLETED/replacement B; Visual has none. `CleanupPhaseEvidence={version:1,identity,phase,startedAt,endedAt,status,failureCode,priorPhaseSha256,calls,purgeCompletions,retiredAttempts,finalResidues,proofHashes}` exists only as the terminal record of its phase log; primary priorPhaseSha256 is null, recovery byte-verifies and names the complete terminal primary-log Sha256. `proofHashes={preDeleteRows,userDelete,postDeleteRows,retainedDoAllowlist}` contains Sha256/null only for fact files first created by that phase, and each final fact file appears nonnull in exactly one phase. Calls are the complete owner trace made by that phase. RetiredAttempts/finalResidues are nonempty only in the one phase that first creates retainedDoAllowlist and they byte-match that proof; earlier candidate residues are not persisted as final. A recovery after user deletion has zero calls/purgeCompletions/retirements/residues, preserves the terminal primary log byte-for-byte, and first creates only the recovery post-delete proof.
- For RetiredAttempt, “canonical sanitized entries” means only the exact LifecycleTerminalEvent, later LifecycleStartEvent, and FinalResidue schemas above serialized by their declared hash rule; no exchange, frame, diagnostic, client observation, or structurally similar arbitrary object qualifies.
- Each irreversible D1 cleanup mutation has a create-once pre-dispatch journal written and fsynced before the call: `CleanupMutationJournal={version:1,operation:'delete_retired_cook_session_indexes'|'delete_disposable_user',operationKeySha256,identity,targets,preStateSha256,preparedAt}`. `targets` is the exact BINARY-sorted retired tuple set or singleton user id; `preStateSha256` hashes the canonical proven-present rows, and the unique disposable identity plus owner trace proves no competing authorized deleter. `ProjectionRetirementReceipt={operation:'delete_retired_cook_session_indexes',at,journalPath,journalSha256,disposition:'deleted'|'reconciled',deletedAttempts,deletedRows,remainingRows}` is no-extra-fields; deletedAttempts is the sorted exact reportAttempts-minus-purgeTargets set selected by RetiredAttempt, remainingRows is zero, deleted requires deletedRows equal its length from the first returned transaction, and reconciled requires deletedRows zero only after a lost response, byte-valid journal/pre-state proof, and an exact read proving every target absent. The scoped runner validates userId and every retired recipeId/attemptId against their canonical identifier grammars before SQL construction, quotes each accepted value through the existing `sqlString` helper, and runs one transaction whose DELETE predicates exact userId, exact retired tuples, and terminal status before returning `changes()` plus the same-user remaining count; no raw caller value is interpolated. Lifecycle receipt is exactly A with deleted/1/0 or reconciled/0/0; Visual is empty with deleted/0/0 and never fabricates reconciliation. `CleanupPreDeleteRows={version:1,phase,identity,at,projectionRetirement,userRows:1,cookSessionIndexRows:0}`; `CleanupUserDelete={version:1,phase,identity,at,journalPath,journalSha256,disposition:'deleted'|'reconciled',deletedUserRows}` where deleted is exactly one returned row and reconciled is exactly zero only after response loss plus byte-valid journal/pre-state and exact user absence; `CleanupPostDeleteRows={version:1,phase,identity,at,userRows:0,productRowCounts}`; `CleanupRetainedDoAllowlist={version:1,phase,identity,at,residues}`. Journals precede their calls; result proofs are create-once after returned-or-reconciled observation and before the next irreversible step. Recovery byte-verifies and reuses every existing journal/proof, may derive only the exact reconciled outcome from its prepared pre-state plus target absence, and never overwrites or relabels it. Product counts equal `CLEANUP_USER_ROW_ITEMS` and are all safe-integer zero. `CleanupOutcomeProof={version:1,identity,passes,phaseEvidence,proofs}` is written atomically last only for a complete clean set; phaseEvidence is exact ordered `{phase,path,sha256}[]`, proofs is exact `{preDeleteRows:{path,sha256},userDelete:{path,sha256},postDeleteRows:{path,sha256},retainedDoAllowlist:{path,sha256}}`, every hash byte-matches, and passes byte-equals summaries derived from immutable phase files. The union of phase calls/completions/retirements/residues is canonical and complete. Final residues byte-equal retained residues; each PurgeCompletion precedes retained.at, then `retained.at <= projectionRetirement.at <= preDelete.at < userDelete.at < postDelete.at <=` the terminal passed phase endedAt. Every final residue satisfies allowed metadata/live-zero; A retirement cross-links terminal/replacement/live-zero evidence plus the exact projection-retirement journal/receipt, pre-delete CookSessionIndex zero, and post-delete ownership zero without any cook-session DELETE A; B has exact terminal DELETE 204. Any owner call at/after userDelete.at rejects evidence. No asserted no-post-delete field exists. For a valid outcome the parser derives the five clean flags, cleanupRecovered exactly from primary-failed/recovery-passed with recovery post-delete proof, and cleanupIncomplete false. A terminal failed phase or missing/incomplete facts produces only sanitized diagnostic smoke output with cleanupIncomplete true and no outcome envelope/Release Cleanup. Unit33/37 additionally require the exact primary-only six-file set, primary passed, and both recovery flags false. Fault tests lose each D1 response after commit and require truthful reconciled proof. Any extra/alias, mutable/hash mismatch, nonfinite error text, pass/phase/provenance inconsistency, schema/registry mismatch, identity/attempt mismatch, false order, missing terminal-204 target completion/A retirement/projection journal/receipt, non-target DELETE, residue mismatch, unexpected count, post-delete owner call, or release construction from incomplete evidence rejects Cleanup. Exact target/pre-state replacement: delete-retired uses BINARY `(recipeId,attemptId,status)` sorted `DeleteRetiredTarget` and same-order `DeleteRetiredPreStateRow={userId,recipeId,attemptId,status,updatedAt}`; delete-user uses singleton `DeleteUserTarget={userId}` and `DeleteUserPreStateRow={userId}`. Compact exact-field-order row-array bytes have no LF and exclude every credential/email/OAuth/profile/content column. preStateSha256 hashes those bytes; operationKeySha256 hashes compact `{operation,identitySha256,targets,preStateSha256}`.
- Cleanup mutation journals are records inside existing `cleanup-phase-<phase>.json`, not additional output files. Exact `CleanupPhaseRecord` is `{kind:'mutation_journal',journal:CleanupMutationJournal}` or `{kind:'terminal',evidence:CleanupPhaseEvidence}` and exact `CleanupPhaseLog={version:1,identity,phase,records:CleanupPhaseRecord[]}`. The file is compact canonical JSON in that field order with no final LF. Before each irreversible call, the runner appends one journal record semantically by writing/fsyncing a complete token-qualified sibling candidate containing the exact prior record prefix plus the one new record, atomically renaming, fsyncing the parent, and byte-reading it before dispatch. After returned/reconciled results and fact files, it similarly appends exactly one terminal record as the final record; a terminal log is immutable. Records permit zero to two mutation journals in operation order followed by exactly one terminal record, or a nonterminal prefix during recovery; duplicate/reordered/changed committed prefixes, foreign/multiple candidates, terminal-not-last, mutation after terminal, and corrupt main fail closed. A same-token partial candidate beside an intact prior main is removed and the extension rebuilt because dispatch is forbidden before main readback; immutable journal plus fact proofs reconstructs a deterministic terminal extension after a dispatched effect. Every `journalPath` is that phase file and `journalSha256` hashes compact canonical bytes of the nested CleanupMutationJournal only, while the phase Artifact hash covers complete terminal CleanupPhaseLog bytes. Recovery faults every candidate write/fsync/rename/readback boundary and either promotes the one complete prefix extension, removes an absent/zero-byte owned candidate, or, only for foreign/multiple/wrong-token/corrupt-main state, fails closed. The existing six cleanup basenames and 14/38-file closed sets remain exact.
- `CLEANUP_USER_ROW_ITEMS` is the immutable sorted exact set `api/auth rows`, `cook session index rows`, `cookbook/membership rows`, `notification/device rows`, `recipe/child/cover rows`, `save/tag/search rows`, `shopping rows`, `spoon/social rows`, and `user rows`. `shopping rows` explicitly includes `ShoppingListItemSyncTombstone`. Each named query aggregates every current or planned D1 table in that ownership family reachable directly or transitively from identity.userId; config tests fail when a migration/model adds such a table without updating the registry and its zero-row query. Smoke and visual fixtures create no R2 object; the pre/post broad `--assert-clean` gates independently prove the global disposable R2 set zero.
- Exact evidence objects are: unit32 `{unit:"unit32",reviewers:Reviewer[]}`; unit33 `{unit:"unit33",deploymentsBefore:Deployment[],cleanupReconcile:CleanupReconcile,deploymentsAfter:Deployment[],newDeploymentIds:string[],qaDeployDisposition:"created"|"existing"|"reconciled",healthSamples:Health[],smokeArtifactPaths:string[],cleanup:Cleanup}`; unit34 `{unit:"unit34",prUrl,prNumber,prHeadSha,prDisposition:"created"|"existing"|"reconciled",reviewers:Reviewer[]}`; unit35 `{unit:"unit35",prHeadSha,branchProtectionStrict,branchProtectionLinearHistory,protectedCheckNames:string[],mandatoryCheckNames:string[],checks:Check[]}`; unit36 `{unit:"unit36",qaHealthSamples:Health[],productionDeploymentsBefore:Deployment[],mergeMethod:"squash",mergeDisposition:"created"|"existing"|"reconciled",squashCommit:SquashCommit}`; unit37 `{unit:"unit37",ciWorkflow:CiWorkflow,workflowCandidates:Workflow[],selectedWorkflow:Workflow,deployJob:DeployJob,releaseArtifactPath,productionRelease:ProductionRelease,productionDeploymentsAfter:Deployment[],newProductionDeploymentIds:string[],healthSamples:Health[],cleanupReconcile:CleanupReconcile,smokeArtifactPaths:string[],visual:Visual,visualReviewers:VisualReviewer[],continuation:Continuation,cleanup:Cleanup}`. Every disposition byte-equals its ensure outcome and obeys intent rules. Passed-stage validation requires exact reviewer roles, schedules, set differences, and SHAs; Unit33 requires passed QA CleanupReconcile before broad cleanup/fresh smoke; Unit35 strict/linear protection plus mandatory success; Unit36 exact squash SHA/parent/tree. Unit37 requires its embedded continuation to byte-equal the separately retained continuation artifact, bind the same source/tree/merge/PR identity, report exact open counts from its arrays, and set ready true; Unit37 requires exact-merge CI success, sorted/frozen workflow candidates, terminal selected Workflow and DeployJob success, release/health equality, a passed CleanupReconcile covering every current-identity or ancestry-authorized failed cleanup diagnostic, exact Visual evidence, and two distinct passed/hash-valid VisualReviewers. Both Cleanup objects derive all clean flags true and recovery/incomplete false; every path is hashed and no field claims all DO metadata absent.
- Unit32 begins by fetch/integrate origin/main, finishes every tracked code/doc/progress change, writes and pushes the final task-local AUTOPILOT release-transfer snapshot, then sets testedBaseSha to exact origin/main, branchHeadSha to that clean/pushed HEAD, and branchHeadTreeSha to exact `HEAD^{tree}` before local/QA gates. It performs exact one-time manifest initialization or proven crash recovery, appends the execution-contract schema ReleaseRun and unit32 StageRun, and executes `release-continuity-transfer` as that stage's first required logical command before any local-validation command. The exact transfer-continuity adapter only validates and returns ready; its enclosing finish-command creates release-continuity JSON plus its immutable receipt from the post-transition revision/time; from its success onward all Unit32-37 continuity/status/checklist/progress updates go only to release-evidence manifest/release-continuity JSON, with task.md changed only for lifecycle transitions, and never to tracked repository files. If integration or any later fix changes HEAD, supersede evidence, update the tracked transfer snapshot before the next freeze when needed, and restart Unit32. Same-HEAD transient retry appends StageRun; crash resumes through the interruption rules above. Any code/HEAD/tree change terminalizes the active stage, marks ReleaseRun superseded, and appends a new run only after Unit32 setup. At Unit35 require live main branch protection `strict:true` and `required_linear_history.enabled:true`. Unit36 executes the exact `fetch-protection-drift` adapter to refetch/reread origin/main and both protections; any base change or protection mismatch supersedes and loops integration plus Units32-35. With exact unchanged base/head, only frozen `merge-ensure` may invoke the guarded squash child, with no merge/rebase/admin fallback. Strict protection is the server-side base-race guard: a concurrently advanced base must reject the squash and trigger the same loop. An interrupted merge attempt with intent can only reconcile the exact SquashCommit; absent/unknown state fails closed without another mutation. No evidence is overwritten.
- After each Unit32-37 StageRun becomes failed or passed, update persisted manifest revision/time plus release-continuity and commit/push complete Desk evidence before another stage/retry. The one mid-release lifecycle change is the journaled first-PR transition, whose product doing commit supersedes/loops the run before recapture. Thereafter tracked product docs stay immutable; task/Desk doing/track change again only in DeskArchive. Ordinary running state is local except pushed ensure arm/dispatch checkpoints: another host may win a pre-dispatch handoff and retain the same root authority, while after dispatch it may observe effect in memory but cannot certify absence or mutate evidence. Unit37 pushes passed active evidence, then release-terminal alone owns host-bound cleanup, mode-specific task closure, move, and final validation.
- Remote side-effect recovery is exact: QA ensure reads exact branchHeadSha deployment plus health; PR ensure reads the sole open/merged PR for head branch+SHA; merge ensure reads PR state plus exact SquashCommit; production reads the exact mergeSha CI `push` run, resulting production `workflow_run`, promoted source/tree canary artifact, and canonical health. Older failed/interrupted attempts can precede a pass only through the ensure intent/disposition rules and latest successful required attempts. At Unit34 the caller brief states that this execution/doing contract overrides Work Merger's generic merge-method, cleanup, and tracked continuity/progress defaults: the invocation may perform its initial fetch/integration loop, but after PR review it must skip the generic merge-first/fallback command and execute only Unit36's exact squash ensure; it must defer generic remote/local branch and worktree cleanup until Unit37; and every required Arc/AUTOPILOT update must target task-root release-evidence manifest/release-continuity JSON, with Desk task.md changed only for lifecycle transitions rather than the frozen tracked files. The same single invocation owns production validation, deployed production visual dogfood, and Desk closure.
- After Unit37 pass/finish-run/pushed active validation, terminal cleanup runs outside ProcessCommand on the frozen executionHost. Before validator creation it writes/pushes exact no-extra-fields `TerminalCleanupAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,branchHeadSha,executionHost,canonicalRepoPath:'/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2',validatorRuntimePath,validatorRuntimeTempPath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveTempPath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,worktreePath,worktreeDeletePath,worktreeCleanupSha256,branch,phase,activeCommand,commandResults,originMainContainsMerge,canonicalMainContainsMerge,validatorReady,worktreeAbsent,registeredWorktreeAbsent,localBranchAbsent,remoteBranchAbsent,pruned,startedAt,updatedAt}`. `worktreePath=identity.repoCwd`, `branch=identity.branch`, and `branchHeadSha` is the identity-bound release head; repaired closure uses the predecessor identity for original ancestry/ref/worktree cleanup without inventing `identity.worktreePath` or `identity.branchHeadSha`. Initial prepared has attemptOrdinal 1, empty priorFailedAttemptPaths with the hash of exact `[]`, and null worktreeCleanupSha256. Every later prepared attempt has the next ordinal and BINARY-sorted immutable prior failure paths/set hash. Prepared freezes final/token-qualified temp and worktree-delete sibling paths, has null validator hashes, `activeCommand:null`, and `commandResults:[]`; hashes become nonnull exactly at validator_ready after source/tree/blob/lockfile verification against validatorMergeSha, archive creation, install, and atomic rename. Normal validatorMergeSha=mergeSha; repaired closure uses the immutable repair leaf receipt's validatorMergeSha while original mergeSha remains the cleanup identity. Phases, active-command/result transitions, commandResults, and booleans remain monotonic; canonical main may be a clean nondivergent descendant and is never rewound.
- The TerminalCleanup phase has one closed no-shell command registry and no unregistered subprocess in that phase. Let `C=/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2`, `W=attempt.worktreePath`, `B=attempt.branch`, and `H=attempt.branchHeadSha`. Exact ordered names/argv/cwd are: `fetch-origin`: `["git","fetch","--prune","origin"]` in W; `origin-contains-merge`: `["git","merge-base","--is-ancestor",mergeSha,"origin/main"]` in W; `canonical-fast-forward`: `["git","merge","--ff-only","origin/main"]` in C; `canonical-contains-merge`: `["git","merge-base","--is-ancestor",mergeSha,"HEAD"]` in C; `validator-tree`: `["git","rev-parse",validatorMergeSha+"^{tree}"]` in W; `validator-members`: `["git","ls-tree","-r","--full-tree",validatorMergeSha]` in W; `archive`: `["git","archive","--format=tar","--output",validatorArchiveTempPath,validatorMergeSha]` in W; `archive-members`: `["tar","-tf",validatorArchiveTempPath]` in W; `extract`: `["tar","-xf",validatorArchiveTempPath,"-C",validatorRuntimeTempPath]` in W; `install`: `["pnpm","install","--frozen-lockfile"]` in validatorRuntimeTempPath; `worktree-list-before`: `["git","worktree","list","--porcelain"]` in C; `local-ref-before`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/heads/"+B]` in C; `remote-ref-before`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/remotes/origin/"+B]` in C; `worktree-detach`: `["mv","--",W,attempt.worktreeDeletePath]` in C; `worktree-prune`: `["git","worktree","prune","--expire","now"]` in C; `worktree-list-after`: `["git","worktree","list","--porcelain"]` in C; `local-ref-delete`: `["git","update-ref","-d","refs/heads/"+B,H]` in C; `local-ref-after`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/heads/"+B]` in C; `remote-ref-delete`: `["git","push","origin","--force-with-lease=refs/heads/"+B+":"+H,":refs/heads/"+B]` in C; `final-fetch`: `["git","fetch","--prune","origin"]` in C; `remote-ref-after`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/remotes/origin/"+B]` in C. The before probes must exit zero: worktree-list-before contains exactly one canonical record for W at H on B, and both ref probes equal H; the after worktree probe must omit W and both after `rev-parse --verify --quiet` ref probes must exit one with empty stdout/stderr, which is the registry-defined successful-absence observation. `ls-tree` parses strict mode/type/object/tab/path rows, rejects links/submodules/path traversal/duplicate paths, and must equal the BINARY-sorted non-directory archive-member list; archive directory entries must be trailing-slash exact prefixes of at least one source path; `rev-parse` accepts one lowercase 40-hex line. Archive SHA-256, extracted regular-file SHA-256, lockfile equality, source-member equality, and canonical manifest hashes use in-process typed filesystem/crypto adapters over regular files only, compact canonical JSON, BINARY path order, and no final LF; they spawn no hidden command. Every invocation first pushes/readbacks exact no-extra-fields `TerminalCommandIntent={sequence,name,argv,cwd,timeoutMs,preStateSha256,preparedAt,recoveryObservations}` as activeCommand with `recoveryObservations:[]`, then after observation atomically appends exact no-extra-fields `TerminalCommandResult={sequence,name,argv,cwd,timeoutMs,preStateSha256,postStateSha256,outcome,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount,recoveryObservations,completedAt}` copies the exact append-only activeCommand.recoveryObservations into the result and clears activeCommand before return/advance where recoveryObservations is empty except for the remote-ref-delete specialization and sequence is its zero-based registry index, name/argv/cwd/timeout match that index, warningCount is a nonnegative safe integer and must be zero to advance, and outcome is `exit|signal|timeout_term|timeout_kill|spawn_error|reconciled`. Exit has integer exitCode 0..255 and null signal; signal has null exitCode and signal `SIGHUP|SIGINT|SIGQUIT|SIGABRT|SIGKILL|SIGALRM|SIGTERM|SIGUSR1|SIGUSR2|SIGPIPE`; timeout_term/timeout_kill have null exitCode and SIGTERM/SIGKILL respectively; spawn_error has both null and empty-stream hashes; reconciled has both null, empty-stream hashes, warningCount zero, and is legal only for a mutation whose exact postStateSha256 is observed after a crash before result persistence. Only registry-defined successful-absence exit one or exit zero is success. Streams are clean UTF-8/NUL-free/sanitized and capped at 1048576 bytes; environment is exactly `PATH=/opt/homebrew/bin:/usr/bin:/bin`, `HOME=/Users/arimendelow`, `USER=arimendelow`, `LOGNAME=arimendelow`, `LANG=C`, `LC_ALL=C`, `CI=1`, `NO_COLOR=1`, `FORCE_COLOR=0`, `GIT_TERMINAL_PROMPT=0`, all other keys unset. Timeout is 600000ms for install, 120000ms for fetch/archive/extract/remote deletion, and 60000ms otherwise, with process-group TERM/5000ms/KILL/reap. `commandResults` is the immutable contiguous registry prefix: every success or failure is persisted if storage remains writable, a failed final entry prevents later entries within that attemptOrdinal until TerminalFailureDisposition authorizes a new ordinal, and no result may be removed/reordered/replaced. Recovery validates the exact prefix, optional activeCommand, and each command's canonical pre/post state. A read-only active command reruns. A mutating active command reruns only when exact preStateSha256 still holds; if exact postStateSha256 holds it appends a reconciled result without fabricating process streams; any other or ambiguous state blocks. Remote-ref-delete is the sole response-loss specialization: after its process group is proven dead, before ordinary success finalization and on every recovery with that active command, run exact read-only `remote-ref-delete-observe=["git","ls-remote","--exit-code","--heads","origin","refs/heads/"+B]` in C. Persist/push/readback exact no-extra-fields `TerminalRecoveryObservation={name:'remote-ref-delete-observe',argv,cwd,outcome:'present'|'absent',remoteSha,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,observedAt}` by appending it to activeCommand.recoveryObservations; present requires exit zero, one exact `H<TAB>refs/heads/B` line and remoteSha H, while absent requires exit two, empty streams, and remoteSha null. Absent reconciles the prior deletion without another push; present H alone permits exact lease-guarded retry; any other exit/SHA/stream is a typed terminal failure. No mutation retries under weaker authority. Alternate argv/cwd/env, shell use, short write, unexpected probe value, remote lease loss, changed object/member/hash, remote observation, warning, or postcondition mismatch fails closed.
- Terminal command journaling is closed under crashes. activeCommand is null or exactly the next registry entry; it is pushed/read back before process spawn and must be null at every phase-advance checkpoint and in final TerminalCleanup. Canonical state hashing covers every command-specific observable needed to distinguish untouched prestate from complete intended poststate, including refs, worktree registration/path, canonical HEAD, archive/runtime manifests, and remote tracking state. A crash after mutation but before result persistence therefore yields either exact prestate, exact poststate, or a hard failure; recovery never invents an exit code, signal, stdout, or stderr. Tests fault before spawn, after every mutating syscall/process completion, before result append, and at each push/readback.
- Worktree removal never uses recursive `git worktree remove`. Before registry command worktree-detach, release-terminal pushes/readbacks exact task-artifact path `artifacts/terminal-worktree-cleanup/attempt.v1.json` containing `TerminalWorktreeCleanupAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,worktreePath,deletePath,manifest,manifestSha256,phase,nextDeleteIndex,startedAt,updatedAt}` with phase `prepared|detached|unregistered|deleting|complete`. `deletePath` is an absent token-qualified sibling on the same filesystem. Its complete no-extra-fields `WorktreeMember={relativePath,kind:'file'|'directory'|'symlink',sha256}[]` uses the same no-follow/hash/order rules as TerminalResourceMember. worktree-detach is one atomic rename; exact source absence plus hash-valid deletePath reconciles response loss. worktree-prune and worktree-list-after advance unregistered only after registration absence. Then the typed filesystem adapter deletes members in deterministic reverse-depth/BINARY order, persisting nextDeleteIndex; a crash after deletion but before advance reconciles an expected missing member, while unexpected type/hash/link/path fails closed. Complete requires source/delete path and registration absent and atomically becomes immutable task artifact `artifacts/terminal-worktree-cleanup/receipt.v1.json`; its hash populates TerminalCleanupAttempt.worktreeCleanupSha256 before worktree_pruned. Fault every rename/prune/member/receipt boundary. The later local/remote ref commands cannot start until this receipt is pushed/read back.
- Terminal work after passed Unit37 has its own total failure lifecycle and never mutates the passed StageRun/ReleaseRun. Exact immutable task-artifact `TerminalFailureDisposition={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,unit37StageRun,terminalPhase,sourceAttemptPath,sourceAttemptSha256,attemptOrdinal,commandMode,terminalCode,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,retryOrdinal,classification,maxRetries,repairCode,createdAt}` has terminalPhase `terminal_cleanup|archive_validation|resource_cleanup|desk_archive|track_archive|repair_index`, commandMode `process|filesystem|git`, and classification `retry_terminal|external_wait|human_blocker|repair_successor`. Exact `TerminalCode` is `credential_missing|billing_required|platform_capability_missing|github_rate_limited|github_5xx|dns_failure|network_timeout|eventual_consistency|cleanup_incomplete|spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal|warning|output_invalid|schema_invalid|validation_failed|configuration_failed|provenance_failed`. Its classification table is total: credential/billing/platform -> human_blocker/0; rate-limit/5xx/DNS/network/eventual/spawn/timeout/signal -> retry_terminal/maxRetries 2 at ordinals 1..2 and external_wait at 3+; cleanup_incomplete -> retry_terminal twice then repair_successor/cleanup; warning|output_invalid|schema_invalid|validation_failed -> repair_successor/production_validation; configuration_failed -> repair_successor/configuration; provenance_failed -> repair_successor/provenance. Phase derivation is also total: terminal_cleanup maps exact typed credential/provider/network/process outcomes first, registry output/exit/postcondition mismatch to validation_failed, argv/environment/config mismatch to configuration_failed, and ref/tree/member/hash authority mismatch to provenance_failed; archive_validation maps typed process transients first and every cleanly observed nonzero/schema/hash semantic rejection to validation_failed; resource_cleanup maps retryable injected I/O to cleanup_incomplete and unexpected member/type/hash/link/path to provenance_failed; desk_archive|track_archive|repair_index consume ordinary rejected-push winner convergence without a disposition, map retryable fetch/push transport failures to network_timeout or github_5xx as observed, schema/tree/ancestry/hash mismatch to provenance_failed, and local argv/environment/config failure to configuration_failed. Raw generic exit or filesystem error is never a TerminalCode: the named phase/command adapter must produce exactly one row above before persistence. Unknown/overlapping tuples reject. The same normal/repaired release-terminal invocation derives and pushes this disposition before returning its exact waiting/blocked/successor result; callers cannot supply a classification. `TerminalWaitCheckpoint={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,terminalPhase,sourceDispositionPath,sourceDispositionSha256,waitOrdinal,scheduleSeconds,retryAfterSeconds,delaySeconds,notBefore,createdAt}` and exact sibling `TerminalWaitResolution={version:1,checkpointPath,checkpointSha256,resolutionEvidencePath,resolutionEvidenceSha256,resolvedAt}` reuse the capped schedule and read-only availability probe. Exact `TerminalBlockerResolution={version:1,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,resolutionEvidencePath,resolutionEvidenceSha256,resolvedAt}` is legal only after the blocked capability probe succeeds. Reinvoking the same normal/repaired terminal command before notBefore or while blocked returns the same immutable progress result with zero mutation; at/after notBefore it either appends the next wait or writes the wait resolution, and a newly available blocker writes blocker resolution. A resolution returns the exact resolved progress branch and the immediately following identical invocation enters the authorized next ordinal. Resolution resumes terminal work only on the frozen executionHost, not a StageRun; foreign hosts validate/read but never mutate. Before every disposition, release-terminal creates immutable BINARY task-relative `artifacts/terminal-failures/<terminalPhase>/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>-snapshot.v1.json` from the exact failure-time attempt bytes and sourceAttemptPath/sourceAttemptSha256 name/hash that snapshot. For TerminalCleanup or ArchiveValidation, retry_terminal atomically consumes the failed active attempt into that snapshot, retains disposition/evidence, and creates only the next ordinal attempt from exact current state. For resource/Desk/track/index journals, the snapshot is immutable while the active journal stays at the same phase; retry_terminal may repeat only the exact idempotent operation from proven prestate, and exact poststate reconciles. The new attempt's priorFailedAttemptPaths/set hash include every immutable predecessor. Its commandResults begins with the longest contiguous successful prefix copied byte-for-byte from the immediately prior snapshot; every copied result must match that snapshot's same sequence and the current state must satisfy the registry's monotonic invariant, but historical read-only output is never re-observed or relabelled. The prior failed entry is omitted, then reruns only from exact prestate or becomes reconciled from exact poststate; ambiguous state routes repair/block rather than fabrication. TerminalCleanupAttempt and ArchiveValidationAttempt use ordinal/prior-failure fields; their failed ordinal is immutable but does not absorb later authorized attempts. Other terminal schemas remain unchanged and bind their disposition history through immutable failure snapshots. repair_successor initializes the measured successor coordinator with `dispositionKind:'terminal'`, the passed Unit37 stage run, and the terminal disposition; after reviewed implementation/Units32-37/merge/index, repaired release-terminal resumes/closes the predecessor using the repair-leaf validator SHA. The predecessor remains terminal-pending, cannot notify Slugger, and preserves every failed attempt/disposition as manifest-closed artifacts until root closure. Tests enumerate every phase/code/retry boundary, wait, blocker, successor, crash, and exact no-extra-fields result.
- Terminal cleanup is host-bound and follows the exact phase/null/result-prefix matrix. Every attempt phase permits only the commandResults prefix ending at or before that phase's last registry command; every phase advance requires its complete successful prefix. Final TerminalCleanup preserves the complete 21-entry commandResults array, includes both mergeSha and validatorMergeSha, and has all terminal booleans true. Another host may read and schema-validate the pushed journal bytes but runs no terminal command and records no phase mutation; it cannot append to the host-bound journal. Resume accepts only the exact phase-specific filesystem/ref state and command prefix; monotonic same-identity winners converge and every command, phase, failure, crash, race, and receipt boundary is fault-tested.
- The active non-artifact ordinary set is exact seven files below identity.taskSourcePath: `task.md`, `release-continuity.v1.json`, the four `{feedback-source,planning,doing,continuity}.md` mirrors in dirname(identity.deskDoingPath), and that iteration's `artifacts/.gitkeep`. Root `artifacts/.gitkeep` is artifact infrastructure. Artifacts otherwise equal the manifest-closed files. Immediately before DeskArchive, ordinary-normal has exactly `terminal-cleanup.v1.json` as its terminal protocol; repair-successor-normal has exactly `terminal-cleanup.v1.json` plus the already-frozen `post-merge-repair.v1.json`. Repair-intermediate and repair-root closures use their separately defined PredecessorSupersede paths rather than DeskArchive. Unknown ordinary/protocol/lookalike/temp/attempt files reject.
- Desk archival begins only from identity task/track validating, passed TerminalCleanup, and no validating attempt. Before lifecycle mutation it writes/fsyncs/pushes active-root `desk-archive.attempt.v1.json`. `ArchiveOrdinaryFile={path,sha256}` is exact with normalized identity-task-relative regular-file path, SHA-256, BINARY sort, and unique path. `DeskArchiveAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,task,sourcePath,targetPath,trackPath,doingPath,prNumber,prUrl,mergeSha,terminalCleanupSha256,lifecycleAt,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,ordinaryFiles,phase,taskDone,doingDone,trackDone,sourceAbsent,targetPresent,archiveValid,startedAt,updatedAt}` requires task/source/target/track/doing byte-equal ReleaseTaskIdentity; phase is `prepared|lifecycle_done|root_moved|archive_validated`, booleans monotonic, immutable fields frozen, and every checkpoint uses the Git matrix. Prepared precomputes task validating->done, lifecycle timestamp, cleared active iteration, matching merged PR/history; Desk doing VALIDATING->COMPLETE; and a semantic transform removing only the identity target row and inserting its exact Landed row while preserving unrelated rows/order. Concurrent unrelated rows rebase; identity target drift or duplicate Landed fails closed. ordinaryFiles is exact branch-specific closed-set hashes. Recovery accepts only before/done bytes, reparses/reapplies the transform, then exact git mv. Final `DeskArchive` repeats every immutable field with terminal booleans true; attempt unlink plus receipt commit/push is atomic.
- The exact inserted track block is rendered from ReleaseTaskIdentity as `## Landed\n\n| Slug | State | Repos | Tracker link | Doing doc |\n|------|-------|-------|--------------|-----------|\n| \`<identity.task>\` | done | spoonjoy-v2 (local) | <prUrl> @ \`<mergeSha>\` | \`taskdoc:spoonjoy-v2/<identity.task>/<relative iteration directory>/doing.md\` |\n\n`; `<relative iteration directory>` is dirname(identity.deskDoingPath) after removing identity.taskSourcePath, normalized by TaskDocumentLocator. The primary identity renders the Clem row; B/C render their own slugs and document locators. The locator is stable across task and whole-track moves and resolves only by the locator contract below; no active/archive physical path may be stored in the row. The block is inserted once immediately before `## Adoption summary`. The active Tasks table retains its header/separator and every unrelated row in order. Task Landed, iteration PR number, Desk doing Merge, and receipt `doingLocator` use the same prNumber/prUrl/mergeSha/document-locator bytes.
- DeskArchive competing-writer convergence is exact. Each phase candidate is clean L atop predecessor O. On rejection fetch R and require R descends O. For task/doing/protocol paths accept only byte-identical unrelated paths or valid monotonic same-identity successor. For track.md parse R, require the target-row precondition or already-applied Landed row, preserve every unrelated valid row, reapply the semantic transform with lifecycleAt, and create a new candidate L2 atop R; full-file hash equality to O is never required for unrelated row changes. After an already-applied phase, a loser L converges with K whose tree is R and parents R,L via commit-tree, normal-pushes only R->K, then ff-only advances. Retry at most eight races. This covers lifecycle, git-mv, candidate validation, receipt/unlink, and validating cancellation.
- After task archive passes, Desk scans one fetched main tree. `remainingUnarchivedTasks` is the BINARY-sorted unique union of every non-underscore task directory still under `spoonjoy-v2/` regardless of lifecycle status and every `spoonjoy-v2/_archive/<task>` child lacking its hash-valid final task-archive receipt (`desk-archive.v1.json` or `predecessor-supersede.v1.json`) or containing a live archive/terminal attempt. Those final receipts prove root_moved/archive-valid task state without depending on the later track-aware ArchiveValidationReceipt, so no cycle exists; lifecycle `done` alone never suffices. `TrackDisposition={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,decision:'kept_active'|'archived',remainingUnarchivedTasks,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,targetPath,trackArchiveSha256,completedAt}` is exact; triggerTask is identity.task, trackGeneration is exact scanDeskSha, targetPath is exact `_archive/spoonjoy-v2/generation-<scanDeskSha>`, kind/hash follow the triggering normal or repaired receipt, kept_active requires nonempty remaining/null archive hash, and archived requires empty remaining/exact TrackArchive hash. Empty scan writes exact `TrackArchiveAttempt={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',sourcePath:'spoonjoy-v2',targetPath,triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,trackBeforeSha256,trackClosedSha256,remainingUnarchivedTasks:[],phase,trackClosed,sourceTreeMoved,targetPresent,archiveValid,startedAt,updatedAt}`; final TrackArchive repeats every immutable field with all terminal booleans true. Target must be absent before prepared; full SHA qualification prevents generation collision.
- Before the successful root_moved push, every fetch/rescan or rejected push that observes any remainingUnarchivedTasks consumes the attempt as kept_active and never moves the root; an empty rescan may rebuild/retry, at most eight. The accepted normal root_moved push from the last empty scan is the archive linearization point. After it, the archived decision is irrevocable: a later newly created `/Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2` is a distinct active track generation with its own future scanDeskSha/target and is preserved, never moved into or merged with the old generation. `sourceTreeMoved:true` describes only the scanned generation and remains true if the source pathname is recreated. Archived task and repair-index locators resolve through the unique hash-valid TrackArchive.targetPath, never a fixed unqualified `_archive/spoonjoy-v2` root.
- Archive closed-set validation uses the phase-specific normal/repaired sets above. Ordinary files/artifacts remain exact and matching attempt/temp files are legal only in their journal phase; final rejects attempts, temps, links, lookalikes, drift, and extras. Final validation runs from the isolated validatorMergeSha runtime with literal `pnpm release:evidence -- validate --manifest <final absolute manifest path> --mode archive`. Exact `ArchiveValidationReceipt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,commandResult,validatedAt}` binds original cleanup SHA plus validator source SHA. Archive validation has its own sole no-shell subprocess: exact argv `["pnpm","release:evidence","--","validate","--manifest",<final absolute manifest path>,"--mode","archive"]`, cwd validatorRuntimePath, the terminal closed environment, timeout 120000ms, and exact no-extra-fields `ArchiveValidationCommandResult={sequence:0,name:'archive-validation',argv,cwd,timeoutMs:120000,outcome,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount}` with the frozen argv/cwd, TerminalCommandResult's finite outcome/null rules, and sanitized capped stream hashes. Exact `ArchiveValidationAttempt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,phase,commandResult,startedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|failed|validated`; ordinal 1 has empty priorFailedAttemptPaths/hash-of-`[]`, and every later ordinal carries the BINARY immutable prior snapshot set: prepared alone has null commandResult; failed has one non-success or positive-warning result and is terminal for that ordinal, then requires TerminalFailureDisposition before another ordinal; validated has exactly exit zero/null signal/zero warnings. The validated attempt plus absent receipt atomically becomes absent attempt plus final receipt carrying that same successful result. Recovery reruns the read-only validator only from prepared/null-result; a recorded failed/validated result is never rerun or replaced within its ordinal; an authorized next ordinal preserves its path/hash in priorFailedAttemptPaths. Receipt push/readback precedes runtime/archive deletion; after receipt, recovery initializes or resumes only the TerminalResourceCleanupAttempt below. Runtime/archive/temp creation and resource cleanup use the injected typed filesystem adapter with parent fsync and no subprocess. Cleanup never follows links; exact journal-owned partial deletion reconciles as specified below, while an unexpected member/type/link target/hash/path fails closed. Overall completion and Slugger require the ordinary-normal or repaired-root final receipt, runtime/archive absence, and pushed disposition; a repair-successor-normal receipt/index is an intermediate terminal handoff and cannot notify.
- Validator runtime/archive deletion is a separate host-bound journaled protocol after ArchiveValidationReceipt push/readback and before terminal result or Slugger preparation. Exact task-root basename `terminal-resource-cleanup.attempt.v1.json` contains no-extra-fields `TerminalResourceCleanupAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorRuntimeDeletePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveDeletePath,validatorArchiveSha256,runtimeManifest,runtimeManifestSha256,phase,nextDeleteIndex,runtimeDetached,archiveDetached,archiveDeleted,startedAt,updatedAt}`. Delete paths are token-qualified siblings frozen before mutation and absent initially. `runtimeManifest` is the complete BINARY-relative-path-sorted no-extra-fields `TerminalResourceMember={relativePath,kind:'file'|'directory'|'symlink',sha256}[]`; file sha256 hashes bytes, symlink sha256 hashes link-target bytes without following it, directory sha256 is null. `phase` is `prepared|runtime_detached|archive_detached|deleting|complete`; prepared requires both originals exact and delete paths absent; runtime_detached atomically renames runtime to its delete path and fsyncs the parent; archive_detached does the same for the archive; deleting removes manifest members in deterministic reverse-depth then BINARY order without following links, persisting nextDeleteIndex after each member, then removes the empty runtime root and exact archive tombstone; complete requires both original and delete paths absent. A crash after rename/delete but before journal advance reconciles only from exact source absence plus hash-valid tombstone/remaining-manifest state; an already-missing next member advances as reconciled, while an unexpected member/type/hash/link/path fails closed. The final Git checkpoint removes the complete attempt only after push/readback of complete and a fresh absence scan. Tests fault after every rename, fsync, member deletion, index write, archive deletion, attempt checkpoint, and final unlink. Foreign hosts never mutate; release completion requires the attempt and all four resource paths absent.
- Slugger is owned by release-terminal only after product/task/track/archive finality. Its sole basename and Desk-repo-relative path are `_meta/notifications/spoonjoy-v2/<identity.repairRootTask>/slugger-notification.v1.json`; its physical path is `/Users/arimendelow/desk/_meta/notifications/spoonjoy-v2/<identity.repairRootTask>/slugger-notification.v1.json`; every eligible ReleaseTerminalResult.sluggerPath byte-equals the relative path. The protocol has one ownership generation and no replacement. Exact no-extra-fields `SluggerNotification={version:1,task:identity.repairRootTask,mergeSha,message,ownershipGeneration:1,writerId,phase,generation,resultPath,resultSha256,completedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|recorded|released|observed|uncertain`; `SluggerSpawnGeneration={generation:1,spawnToken,executionHost,status,gatePath,releasePath,publishPath,resultPath,pid,pgid,processStartIdentity,preparedAt,recordedAt,releasedAt,terminalAt}` has status `prepared|recorded|released|terminal` and the literal monotonic null matrix below. Exact compact canonical no-final-LF bytes are `SluggerGate={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,executionHost,notificationPath,releasePath,publishPath,resultPath,commandSha256,preparedAt}` `SluggerRelease={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,releasedAt}` and host-local `SluggerPublish={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,releaseSha256,publishedAt}`; `notificationDirectory` is exact `/Users/arimendelow/desk/_meta/notifications/spoonjoy-v2/<identity.repairRootTask>`; notificationPath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-notification.v1.json`, gatePath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-generation-1-gate.v1.json`, releasePath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-generation-1-release.v1.json`, and resultPath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-generation-1-result.v1.json`. Those four are the only registered regular non-symlink Desk paths and exact siblings; publishPath is exact `/Users/arimendelow/Library/Caches/spoonjoy-release/<spawnToken>/generation-1-publish.v1.json` under a mode-0700 token directory and is never Git-tracked, commandSha256 hashes compact canonical `SluggerCommandSpec`, and every field equals the journal generation.
