QA reconcile argv also includes `--target-env qa --base-url QB`; production includes `--target-env production`. Unit29.2/30/31 test every operand and identity mismatch.
- Reconcile output policy is exact `cleanup-reconcile`, not one-file `json`. Fresh passed output contains root `cleanup-reconcile.json` plus one `target-<64-lower-hex targetKeySha256>/` per canonical target. `already_clean` target closed set is exactly `cleanup-reconcile-proof.json`. `reconciled` target closed set is exactly seven files: `cleanup-reconcile-proof.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-phase.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-pre-delete-rows.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-user-delete.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-post-delete-rows.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-retained-do-allowlist.json`, and `cleanup-reconcile-outcome.json`. Every file has its exact no-extra-fields schema and cross-hashes the same target key, environment/base, source identity, attempt locator, diagnostic locator/hash, lineage edges, proof chain, operation journal, and immediately prior phase/fact. A failed command has no aggregate; it retains each prior complete target directory unchanged and, for the current target only, exact `cleanup-reconcile-journal.json`, a contiguous prefix of the six non-proof phase/fact/outcome files authorized by journal.phase, and `cleanup-reconcile-failure.json` hashing every retained file. Missing prefix members, later-phase files, proof on failure, partial bytes, extra target/file, or mutation of a complete predecessor directory fails closed.
- Exact `CleanupReconcileProof={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,disposition:'already_clean'|'reconciled',diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,sourceCleanOutcomeLocator,sourceCleanOutcomeSha256,reconcileOutcomePath,reconcileOutcomeSha256,provedAt}` has already_clean with nonnull source outcome and null reconcile outcome, while reconciled has the reverse; all locators/hashes are verified and no other null matrix is legal. Exact aggregate `CleanupReconcile={version:1,attempts:[{targetKeySha256,target,disposition,proofPath,proofSha256}],completedAt}` sorts by canonical target bytes, requires unique full hashes, and points to every current-attempt proof. Input `[]` writes only aggregate `attempts:[]`. `CleanupReconcileFailure={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,journalPath,journalSha256,retainedPaths,retainedSetSha256,terminalCode,failedAt}` is current-identity evidence and never mutates the source diagnostic or a completed target. `retainedPaths` is the BINARY-path-sorted unique array of every complete retained regular file in the failed current-target directory except `cleanup-reconcile-failure.json`; that receipt is required alongside the listed set but excluded to avoid self-reference. `retainedSetSha256` is lowercase SHA-256 of compact canonical JSON with no final LF for the BINARY-path-sorted unique array `[{path,sha256}]`, where each path byte-equals retainedPaths and each hash covers the complete referenced bytes. Duplicate paths, alternate order, omitted/extra listed files, a listed/unlisted directory member other than the failure receipt, partial bytes, self-inclusion, wrong digest, or noncanonical JSON rejects. Tests cover empty, already-clean, fully reconciled, every contiguous crash prefix, every retained-set mutation/order/duplicate, A->B->C lineage/proof separation, cross-environment/base rejection, full-hash collision resistance, canonical comparator equality, and active/task/archive/TrackArchive relocation.
- The six reconciled phase/fact/outcome artifacts and their temporary journal are fully typed. `CleanupReconcileJournal={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,lineageEdges,proofChain,phase,operationKeySha256,preparedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|phase_recorded|pre_delete_recorded|user_delete_recorded|post_delete_recorded|retained_recorded|outcome_recorded`; immutable identity/diagnostic/lineage/proof/operation/prepared fields never change and updatedAt strictly increases. `CleanupReconcilePhase={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,targetEnvironment,targetBaseUrl,sourceIdentitySha256,attemptLocator,diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,phase:'recovery',startedAt,endedAt,status:'passed',failureCode:null,calls,purgeCompletions,mutationJournals,priorPhaseSha256}`; `CleanupReconcilePreDeleteRows={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,userRows:1,cookSessionIndexRows:0,sourceOutcomeLocator,sourceOutcomeSha256}`; `CleanupReconcileUserDelete={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,mutationJournalIndex,mutationJournalSha256,disposition:'deleted'|'reconciled',deletedUserRows}` where mutationJournalIndex selects exactly one immutable no-extra-fields CleanupMutationJournal member of the phase artifact, mutationJournalSha256 hashes that complete canonical member, deleted means one affected row, and reconciled means zero only after an exact absence proof; `CleanupReconcilePostDeleteRows={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,userRows:0,productRowCounts}`; `CleanupReconcileRetainedDoAllowlist={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,residues}`; and `CleanupReconcileOutcome={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,phasePath,phaseSha256,preDeleteRowsPath,preDeleteRowsSha256,userDeletePath,userDeleteSha256,postDeleteRowsPath,postDeleteRowsSha256,retainedDoAllowlistPath,retainedDoAllowlistSha256,relationalProductRowsZero:true,contentBearingDoStateZero:true,identifierBearingDoMetadataRetained,completedAt}`. `calls`, `purgeCompletions`, `productRowCounts`, and `residues` reuse the exact no-extra-fields Cleanup phase types and canonical comparators; identifierBearingDoMetadataRetained equals whether residues is nonempty. The pre-delete prior link names the phase artifact; user-delete names pre-delete; post-delete names user-delete; retained names post-delete. Outcome cross-hashes all five predecessors, CleanupReconcileProof cross-hashes outcome, and the aggregate cross-hashes the proof; no mutable outer CleanupReconcileJournal hash is used as irreversible-call authority. Every object uses the displayed field order, compact canonical JSON, no final LF, canonical times, normalized target-relative paths, exact target/environment/base/source identity, and verified locator/hash/lineage/proof equality. While running, the journal plus artifact set must be the exact contiguous phase prefix: prepared has none; each named `_recorded` phase adds exactly its corresponding file in the order phase, pre-delete, user-delete, post-delete, retained, outcome. After outcome_recorded, one atomic checkpoint creates the hash-valid CleanupReconcileProof and removes the journal, yielding the exact seven-file passed set. A failed checkpoint retains the journal, only its phase-authorized prefix, and the failure receipt; skipped/duplicate/later/missing files, altered prefix bytes, nullability drift, or a proof beside a journal rejects. Tests fault before/after every candidate write, rename, irreversible call, fact write, phase advance, proof creation, and journal deletion.
- Terminal-code derivation gives a validated unresolved cleanup diagnostic precedence over generic process timeout, signal, exit, warning, or output codes, producing `cleanup_incomplete`. The cloudflare-d1 credential-key comparison and every specialized reconcile credential/lineage check occur in executor preflight before start-command, so mismatch produces commandMode preflight, attempt null, and zero manifest/attempt/provider/product mutation.
- Repair successor orchestration is executable through measured release-terminal successor mode. Strict action domain is `prepare|create-task|start-planning|finish-planning|wait-runtime|resume-runtime|record-runtime-probe|record-handoff|start-implementation|finish-implementation|recover`. `prepare` alone requires ordered `--predecessor-manifest M --release-run R --stage-run G --disposition-kind stage|terminal --disposition P`; every later action rejects those flags and resolves authority only from J. Action-specific required flags are: finish-planning `--attempt N --agent-id D --artifacts-json A`; wait-runtime `--kind planner|doer --suite-attempt N`; resume-runtime `--kind planner|doer --wait-ordinal N`; record-runtime-probe `--kind planner|doer --wait-ordinal N --agent-id D --report-json J`; record-handoff `--handoff-json H`; finish-implementation `--attempt N --agent-id D --artifacts-json A --implementation-evidence P`; other actions accept no extra flags. Exact no-extra-fields result union shares `{mode:'successor',action,journalPath,journalSha256,phase}` and adds: prepare nothing; create-task `{taskPath,identityPath,identitySha256}`; start-planning/start-implementation `{skill:'work-planner'|'work-doer',cwd,prompt,planningPath,doingPath,attempt,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt}`; finish-planning `{planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256}`; wait-runtime `{status:'waiting',waitPath,waitSha256,waitOrdinal,notBefore}`; resume-runtime `{status:'probe_required',prompt,promptSha256,probeOrdinal,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt}`; record-runtime-probe is either waiting with the next wait tuple or `{status:'resolved',resolutionPath,resolutionSha256}`; record-handoff `{handoffPath,handoffSha256}`; finish-implementation `{implementationEvidencePath,implementationEvidenceSha256}`; recover `{status:'stable'|'action_required',nextAction}`. Work Merger invokes only the returned skill/cwd/prompt payload, passes no inherited context, waits to the returned deadline, and records the exact agent/artifact result. Every action checkpoints before invocation and validates outputs before phase advance; all results reject extras and every journal mutation uses the Desk Git matrix/push/readback.
- Exact no-extra-fields `PostMergeSuccessorAttempt={version:1,successorKey,predecessorManifest,predecessorReleaseRun,predecessorStageRun,dispositionKind,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,phase,taskPath,identityPath,identitySha256,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,handoffPath,handoffSha256,suiteAttempts,runtimeWaitPaths,runtimeWaitSetSha256,implementationEvidencePath,implementationEvidenceSha256,createdAt,updatedAt}` requires dispositionKind `stage|terminal`; stage binds a failed Unit37 PostMergeFailureDisposition, terminal binds a passed Unit37 stage plus TerminalFailureDisposition. It uses phase `prepared|task_created|planning_running|contract_approved|handoff_recorded|implementation_running|implementation_complete`. Exact `SuccessorSuiteAttempt={kind:'planner'|'doer',ordinal,status:'running'|'interrupted'|'completed',startedAt,deadlineAt,endedAt,agentId,artifacts,artifactSetSha256}` has `artifacts:{path,sha256}[]` BINARY-sorted unique and a 1800000ms deadline. Running has endedAt/agentId/hash null and artifacts empty; interrupted has canonical endedAt, nullable UUID agentId, empty artifacts, null hash; completed has canonical endedAt, UUID agentId, nonempty hash-valid artifacts, and set hash over compact canonical artifacts. At most two interrupted attempts per kind precede successor-journal `SuccessorRuntimeWaitCheckpoint` files at `<successorTaskRoot>/post-merge-successor-waits/<kind>/wait-<ordinal>.v1.json`; those immutable checkpoints and sibling resolutions use the same schedule/Retry-After/probe rules as ExternalWait but do not touch a predecessor StageRun. `runtimeWaitPaths` is append-only and its set hash is null iff empty. Phase matrix is closed: prepared has every task/doc/handoff/implementation field null and empty attempts; task_created adds task/identity only; planning_running adds exactly one latest running planner; contract_approved requires a completed planner plus all planning/doing path/hash fields; handoff_recorded additionally requires handoff path/hash; implementation_running adds exactly one latest running doer; implementation_complete requires completed doer plus implementation path/hash. Recovery validates existing docs/receipts, completes a provable result, interrupts one expired attempt, or resumes a journal wait; it never silently invokes, fabricates availability, or skips a phase.
- The successor doing doc contains implementation-only red/green/verification/reviewer units for the RepairBrief set and explicitly excludes Units32-37. Exact task-relative manifest Artifact `artifacts/post-merge-successor/post-merge-implementation.v1.json` is `PostMergeImplementationEvidence={version:1,successorKey,successorIdentitySha256,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,implementationBaseSha,implementationHeadSha,implementationTreeSha,unitReceiptPaths,unitReceiptSetSha256,reviewReportPaths,reviewReportSetSha256,verificationArtifactPaths,verificationArtifactSetSha256,coverageSummaryPath,coverageSummarySha256,warnings,completedAt}`. Exact `CoverageSummary={version:1,commands,total,changed,artifacts,warningCount,createdAt}` has nonempty `commands:{argv,exitCode:0,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount:0}[]`; exact `CoverageMetricSet={statements:{covered,total,pct:100},branches:{covered,total,pct:100},functions:{covered,total,pct:100},lines:{covered,total,pct:100}}` requires every total positive and covered equal total; `total` is CoverageMetricSet. Exact `ChangedCoverage` is `{kind:'measured',changedExecutablePaths,changedExecutableSetSha256,statements,branches,functions,lines}` or `{kind:'not_applicable',changedExecutablePaths:[],changedExecutableSetSha256,reason:'no_changed_executable_lines'}`. Measured requires a nonempty BINARY-sorted unique path array, its set hash, and the four positive 100% metric members from CoverageMetricSet. Not_applicable requires `changedExecutableSetSha256` equal lowercase SHA-256 of exact bytes `[]` and is legal only when the independently derived CoverageScope.changedExecutablePaths is empty; the diff, independent production executable registry, instrumented registry, intersection, and hashes are retained in the exact seven machine-readable coverage artifacts. Docs/tests/fixtures/generated outputs and `**/*.d.ts` are excluded only by the exact independent path classifier, while executable root configuration such as `vite.config.ts` remains production executable source and must be instrumented when changed. `coverageSummaryPath` is exact task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/coverage/coverage-summary.json`; `artifacts:{path,sha256}[]` is the execution-contract-exact seven-entry subordinate set and hashes each complete machine-readable file; commands/total/changed equal their corresponding artifact payloads. Arrays in implementation evidence are BINARY-sorted unique task-relative paths; every set hash covers compact canonical `{path,sha256}[]`; all implementation-only units are complete; total is 100%; changed is measured 100% or hash-proven not_applicable; warnings and every command warningCount are zero; branch/head/tree are clean, pushed, and exact. finish-implementation appends every closed successor evidence path to the manifest, then writes/pushes/readbacks this receipt at the exact artifact path before implementation_complete. Only then may universal Units32-37 run once for the successor.
- Recursive terminal validation always uses the immutable repair leaf's `validatorMergeSha`; no active clause uses `successorMergeSha` as an independently inferred value. Ordinary, repair-successor, repair-intermediate, and repair-root are the four exact ReleaseTerminalResult fixtures/branches. Every identity-specific adopted iteration, mirror, Landed slug/path, task source/archive path, and repair locator derives from ReleaseTaskIdentity: iteration root is dirname(identity.deskDoingPath), mirrors use the four fixed basenames there, archive relocation replaces identity.taskSourcePath with identity.taskArchivePath, and the Landed row uses identity.task plus the exact TaskDocumentLocator derived from identity.deskDoingPath. A whole-track archived task resolves only as `<TrackArchive.targetPath>/_archive/<slug>` and a repair index only as `<TrackArchive.targetPath>/_repair-index/<key>.json`; fixed `_archive/spoonjoy-v2` paths are invalid.
- Slugger uses only the exact single `SluggerNotification`, embedded `SluggerSpawnGeneration`, and immutable `SluggerProcessResult` schemas above because `ouro msg` exposes no idempotency key. Prepared gate bytes are remote before the one gate starts; recorded PID/PGID/start identity is remote before release; released journal plus release bytes are remote before the already-recorded gate may spawn the child; result bytes and same-host dead/reaped proof precede observed/uncertain. Prepared-with-no-member and synchronous spawn error terminalize that generation explicitly; same-host recovery may release the existing recorded waiting gate, while released recovery never spawns and foreign-host recovery blocks. This proves one ownership generation and at most one live gate/child without claiming Slugger-side deduplication.
- These Round 51 clauses replace every older `startup_failure`, same workflow/job conclusion, raw lifecycle URL ban, sorted checked-id, caller-supplied capability artifact, exhausted-transient repair, six/four-phase successor, `not_needed`/null proof, one-file reconcile, fixed primary Desk/archive path, `successorMergeSha`, three-branch result, indefinitely running agent, direct OAuth-less Cloudflare REST, and Slugger spawn clause.

- Round 52 terminal/archive closure is exact. `TrackArchiveAttempt` basename is `track-archive.attempt.v1.json` at the active track root; final no-extra-fields `TrackArchive` basename is `track-archive.v1.json`, stable locator `track:spoonjoy-v2/track-archive.v1.json`, and sole physical path `<targetPath>/track-archive.v1.json`. It repeats the frozen generation/trigger/kind/hash/source/target/tree fields, has every terminal boolean true, and hash-equals TrackDisposition.trackArchiveSha256. Final task-root resolution is derived from ReleaseTaskIdentity plus hash-valid DeskArchive or PredecessorSupersede and TrackDisposition: kept_active is `spoonjoy-v2/_archive/<slug>`, archived is `<TrackArchive.targetPath>/_archive/<slug>`. `archive-validation.v1.json` is written only at that already-relocated final root; validation never recreates identity.deskTaskRoot. Track receipt, task receipt, manifest, and validator paths resolve through their registered locator domains and one generation only.
- Round 52 terminal closed sets are exact. Ordinary-normal final task has four files: terminal-cleanup, desk-archive, track-disposition, archive-validation. Repair-successor-normal has those four plus post-merge-repair and its external attempt-free index. Repaired-root has exactly five files: terminal-cleanup, post-merge-repair-link, predecessor-supersede, track-disposition, archive-validation, and no relay/index creation. Repaired-intermediate has exactly those five plus post-merge-repair and must create/read back its attempt-free index before the next ancestor. Temporary attempts/candidates are allowed only in their owning phase and absent at terminal validation. Unit29.2's depth-two fixture asserts the six-file intermediate and five-file root independently.
- Round 52 recovery closure is exact. A failed StageRun and every stage-owned disposition/evidence object are permanent bytes; only task-root wait checkpoints, wait resolutions, blocker resolutions, successor-runtime waits, and runtime-probe journals may be appended afterward. Each command result is the exact no-extra-fields union above. Work Merger dispatches every agent probe itself from returned skill/cwd/prompt/deadline bytes, records the returned agent id/report, and never passes a synthetic availability value. Every provider and agent wait can append another checkpoint forever under the capped schedule; a successful receipt restarts the same owning unit, never a hardcoded Unit37. Fault tests cover every write/fsync/rename/manifest/commit/push/readback boundary and all-null/all-nonnull matrices.
- Round 52 process/evidence closure is exact. Seven policies are registered; every deployment capture uses cloudflare-rest; the OAuth bearer crosses the gate only through the consumed one-shot descriptor; ProcessPreflightPublic includes the full public environment and finite proof/probe matrix; capability evidence uses the preflight/process/agent payload union; blocked and resolved capability artifacts are distinct immutable bytes; URL types and deployment source are finite; QA inventory selection is deterministic but noncausal. Unit29.2 rejects every extra field, wrong environment membership, D1 account/database/permission mismatch, unconsumed descriptor, secret sentinel, malformed URL, and capability-code mismatch.
- Round 52 cleanup closure is exact. CleanupRecoveryIdentity, diagnostics, targets, proofs, and facts bind targetEnvironment plus targetBaseUrl. Successor lineage receipt edges and diagnostic/reconcile proofChain are separate typed arrays. Full canonical target bytes define order and the 64-hex target key. Passed already_clean/reconciled and failed-prefix closed sets are those above; successful cleanup removes credentialKeySha256-bearing journal state. Tests cover current identity, A->B->C, active/task archive/whole-track relocation, cross-environment/base/identity attempts, collisions, response loss, every partial write, and zero fresh-user creation before all target proofs plus broad assert-clean.
- Round 52 successor/notification closure is exact. Successor mode has the action grammar/result union, seven stable delivery phases, append-only suite artifact hashes, journal-owned runtime waits, exact Work Planner/Work Doer invocation payloads, complete phase/null matrix, and the measured/not_applicable coverage receipt above. Slugger stores exactly ownershipGeneration 1 with one token/host/PID/PGID/start identity, immutable gate/release/result paths, phase timestamps, and terminal sanitized result in the actual notification schema. Prepared/no-member, synchronous spawn error, recorded waiting gate, released execution, same-host reap, foreign-host block, rejected initial CAS, and strict no-second-generation recovery are all fault-tested.
